href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/how-to-buy-bitcoin/\">comprehensive guide</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div>", "litecoin": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is Litecoin (LTC)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Litecoin (LTC) is a cryptocurrency that was designed to provide fast, secure and low-cost payments by leveraging the unique properties of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/blockchain\">blockchain</a> technology.</p><p>To learn more about this project, check out our deep dive of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/litecoin\">Litecoin</a>.</p><p>The cryptocurrency was created based on the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/bitcoin/\">Bitcoin</a> (BTC) protocol, but it differs in terms of the hashing algorithm used, hard cap, block transaction times and a few other factors. Litecoin has a block time of just 2.5 minutes and extremely low transaction fees, making it suitable for micro-transactions and point-of-sale payments.</p><p>Litecoin was released via an open-source client on GitHub on Oct. 7, 2011, and the Litecoin Network went live five days later on Oct. 13, 2011. Since then, it has exploded in both usage and acceptance among merchants and has counted among the top ten cryptocurrencies by market capitalization for most of its existence.</p><p>The cryptocurrency was created by Charlie Lee, a former Google employee, who intended Litecoin to be a \"lite version of Bitcoin,\" in that it features many of the same properties as Bitcoin\u2014albeit lighter in weight.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of Litecoin?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>As we previously touched on, Litecoin was founded by Charlie Lee, an early cryptocurrency adopter and a name held in high regard in the cryptocurrency industry.</p><p>Charlie Lee, also known as \u201cChocobo,\u201d is an early Bitcoin miner and computer scientist, who was a former software engineer for Google. In addition, Charlie Lee held the role of director of engineering at Coinbase between 2015 and 2017 before moving on to other ventures.</p><p>Today, Charlie Lee is an outspoken advocate of cryptocurrencies and is the managing director of the Litecoin Foundation\u2014a non-profit organization that works alongside the Litecoin Core Development team to help advance Litecoin.</p><p>Besides Lee, the Litecoin Foundation also includes three other individuals on the board of directors: Xinxi Wang, Alan Austin and Zing Yang \u2014 all of which are accomplished in their own right.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes Litecoin Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Behind Bitcoin, Litecoin is the second most popular pure cryptocurrency. This success can be largely attributed to its simplicity and clear utility benefits.</p><p>As of January 2021, Litecoin is one of the most widely accepted cryptocurrencies, and more than 2,000 merchants and stores now accept LTC across the globe.</p><p>Its main benefit comes from its speed and cost-effectiveness. Litecoin transactions are typically confirmed in just minutes, and transaction fees are nearly negligible. This makes it an attractive alternative to Bitcoin in developing countries, where transaction fees may be the deciding factor on which cryptocurrency to support.</p><p>In late 2020, Litecoin also saw the release of the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-mimblewimble\">MimbleWimble</a> (MW) testnet, which is used to test Mimblewimble-based confidential transactions on Litecoin. Once this feature is available on the mainnet, Litecoin users will also benefit from greatly enhanced privacy and fungibility.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many Litecoin (LTC) Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Like most proof-of-work (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/proof-of-work-vs-proof-of-stake\">POW</a>) cryptocurrencies, the amount of Litecoin in circulation gradually increases with each newly mined block.</p><p>As of January 2021, 66.245 million LTC have already been mined out of a total maximum supply of 84 million. The Litecoin Foundation recently estimated it will be well over 100 years until Litecoin reaches full dilution (around the year 2140) \u2014 since the number of LTC mined per block decreases every four years as part of the block reward halving schedule.</p><p>Around 500,000 LTC was instamined on day one after the LTC genesis block was mined and Charlie Lee and presumably other early Litecoin developers were among the first miners.</p><p>Despite this, as a fairly distributed asset, the Litecoin developers or Charlie Lee do not receive any direct profits from the operation of Litecoin\u2014other than anything they may earn as part of the regular mining process.</p><p>When Litecoin listed on several markets in 2011, the Litecoin price hit $0.30. Then, from November to December 2013, it went on a massive bull run, with Litecoin price hitting a high of $44.73. However, the bear market and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/mt-gox\">Mt. Gox hack</a> caused Litecoin prices to crash in 2014, and prices consolidated within the $2 to $4 range for several years. In November and December of 2017, Litecoin price rallied over 500% to $358.34, on the back of the crypto bull market. Litecoin price hit an all-time high in May 2021, in the latest crypto bull run, which saw it reach $386.45 on May 9, 2021.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the Litecoin Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>As a blockchain-based cryptocurrency, Litecoin is secured by incredibly strong cryptographic defenses \u2014 making it practically impossible to crack.</p><p>Like Bitcoin and several other cryptocurrencies, Litecoin uses the PoW <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/consensus\">consensus</a> algorithm to ensure transactions are confirmed quickly and without errors. The combined strength of the Litecoin mining network prevents double-spends and a range of other attacks, while ensuring the network has 100% uptime.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy Litecoin (LTC)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Litecoin is one of the few cryptocurrencies with a wide variety of fiat trading pairs, and can be exchanged for U.S. dollars (USD), Korean won (KRW), euros (EUR) and more when you <a href=\"https://www.binance.com/en/buy-Litecoin\">buy Litecoin</a>. MWEB is \u201cset to be the largest upgrade to the Litecoin network ever, promising to provide fungibility for all, while improving Litecoin's scalability.\u201d MWEB will be an opt-in feature, allowing Litecoin to be the \u201cmost fungible, cash-like, cryptocurrency in the space.\u201d The security and privacy enhancing Taproot upgrade will also be part of the core release.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Some Exchanges Delist LTC After MimbleWimble Upgrade</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-mimblewimble\">MimbleWimble</a> is an upgrade enabling users to achieve much-needed privacy while transacting on the network. The MimbleWimble upgrade was first proposed in November 2019 through a Litecoin Improvement Proposal. At the time, the Litecoin developers aimed to further focus on improving anonymity between senders and receivers.</p><p>Following the MimbleWimble upgrade at Litecoin block 2,257,920, users could opt for moe transaction privacy and explore other benefits, including blocks containing less needless transaction data. More specifically, long transactions are broken down into a single transfer by recording one input-output pair.</p><p>The MimbleWimble Extension Blocks (MWEB) upgrade was successfully activated on May 19, 2022. However, the upgrade puts Litecoin in the crosshairs of regulators who do not take kindly to privacy-capable cryptocurrencies.</p><p>Some effects of the upgrade became rather apparent when several South Korean exchanges started delisting Litecoin from their platforms shortly after the MWEB upgrade went into effect. Upbit, Bithumb, Coinone, Korbit and Gopax have delisted LTC over the MimbleWimble upgrade, due to how it makes it impossible for these companies to adhere to the Act on the Reporting and Use of Specific Financial Transaction Information. Per South Korean regulation, crypto exchanges need to mitigate money laundering and illicit activities at all costs. That means removing any currencies that provide users with additional privacy or anonymity.</p></div></div></div></div></div>", "monero": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is Monero (XMR)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Monero was launched in 2014, and its goal is simple: to allow transactions to take place privately and with anonymity. Even though it\u2019s commonly thought that BTC can conceal a person\u2019s identity, it\u2019s often easy to trace payments back to their original source because blockchains are transparent. On the other hand, XMR is designed to obscure senders and recipients alike through the use of advanced cryptography.</p><p>The team behind Monero say <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-are-privacy-coins\">privacy</a> and security are their biggest priorities, with ease of use and efficiency coming second. It aims to provide protection to all users \u2014 irrespective of how technologically competent they are.</p><p>Overall, XMR aims to allow payments to be made quickly and inexpensively without fear of censorship.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of Monero?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Seven developers were initially involved in creating Monero \u2014 five of whom decided to remain anonymous. There have been rumors that XMR was also invented by <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/who-is-satoshi-nakamoto\">Satoshi Nakamoto</a>, the inventor of Bitcoin.</p><p>XMR\u2019s origins can be traced back to Bytecoin, a privacy-focused and decentralized cryptocurrency that was launched in 2012. Two years later, a member of the Bitcointalk forum \u2014 only known as thankful<em>for</em>today \u2014 forked BCN\u2019s codebase, and Monero was born. They had suggested \u201ccontroversial changes\u201d to Bytecoin that others in the community disagreed with and decided to take matters into their own hands.</p><p>It\u2019s believed that hundreds of developers have contributed to XMR over the years.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes Monero Private?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>Users shouldn't view all privacy cryptocurrencies as interchangeable or equivalent services because they don't all achieve privacy in the same way. For instance, XMR should be considered a technology that, when used properly, obscures user data on the blockchain, making it harder to identify its users.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Gives Monero Value?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The secrecy and anonymity offered by Monero are what most users find valuable. It gives people the freedom to conduct cryptocurrency transactions anytime they want for any purpose without being concerned about being watched by the government, hackers or other outside parties. XMR coins cannot be traced, thus they cannot be blacklisted by businesses for alleged illicit connections.</p><p>Investors who think that demand for privacy will rise in the future, raising the price and total <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/market-capitalization-market-cap-mcap\">market cap</a> of XMR, may find value in Monero in addition to its use as a medium of exchange.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes Monero Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>There are several things that make Monero unique. One of the project\u2019s biggest aims is achieving the greatest level of decentralization possible, meaning that a user doesn\u2019t need to trust anyone else on the network.</p><p>Privacy is achieved through a few distinctive features. Whereas each Bitcoin in circulation has its own serial number, meaning that cryptocurrency usage can be monitored, XMR is completely fungible. By default, details about senders, recipients and the amount of crypto being transferred are obscured \u2014 and Monero advocates says this offers an upper hand over rival privacy coins such as Zcash, which are \u201cselectively transparent.\u201d</p><p>Obfuscation is achieved through the use of ring signatures. Here, past transaction outputs are picked from the blockchain and act as decoys, meaning that outside observers can\u2019t tell who signed it. If Ian was sending 200 XMR to Susan, this amount could also be split into random chunks to add a further level of difficulty.</p><p>To ensure that transactions cannot be linked to one another, stealth addresses are created for every single transaction that are only used once.</p><p>All of these distinctive features have led to XMR being increasingly used for illicit transactions instead of Bitcoin \u2014 especially on darknet markets. Governments around the world, especially the U.S., have also offered hundreds of thousands of dollars to anyone who can crack Monero\u2019s code.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many Monero (XMR) Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Monero is slightly unusual as a token sale wasn\u2019t held for XMR \u2014 and no tokens were premined either. At the time of writing, the circulating supply of XMR stands at 18,188,773.23.</p><p>This cryptocurrency is designed to be resistant to application-specific integrated circuits, which are commonly used for mining new Bitcoin. In theory, this means that it can be possible to mine XMR using everyday computing equipment.</p><p>Overall, there will eventually be a total of 18.4 million XMR in circulation \u2014 and this cap is expected to be reached on May 31, 2022. After this, miners will be incentivized using \u201ctail emissions,\u201d with a small amount of XMR being fed into the system every 60 seconds as a reward. It is believed this approach is more effective than relying on transaction fees.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the Monero Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>One of Monero\u2019s main goals has to prevent centralization \u2014 and this network uses a consensus mechanism called CryptoNight, which is <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/how-to-mine-monero\">based on</a> proof-of-work. This prevents large mining farms from becoming a dominant force.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy Monero (XMR)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>Because of its nature as a privacy coin, XMR isn\u2019t listed on some major exchanges. For example, although you can <a href=\"https://www.binance.com/en/buy-Monero\">buy XMR on Binance</a>, it isn\u2019t supported by Coinbase. As a result, you may need to convert your fiat into Bitcoin and go through a smaller trading platform. This guide<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/how-to-buy-bitcoin/\"> helps explain</a> how you can convert fiat currencies into crypto with ease. As it\u2019s use grows there has been increased interest in the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/monero/xmr/aud/\">XMR to AUD</a> and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/monero/xmr/eur/\">XMR to EUR</a> price pairs.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Mining on Monero</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Monero uses a <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/proof-of-work-pow\">Proof-of-Work</a> algorithm, RandomX, to validate transactions. The method was introduced in November 2019 to replace the former algorithm CryptoNightR. Both were designed to be <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/asic-resistant\">ASIC-resistant</a>.</p><p><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/how-to-mine-monero\">Monero can be mined</a> somewhat efficiently on consumer-grade hardware, such as x86, x86-64, ARM and GPUs, a design decision that was based on Monero's opposition to mining centralization that <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/asic\">ASIC</a> mining creates. However, it has also resulted in Monero's popularity among malware-based non-consensual miners.<sup></sup></p><p>In October of 2021, the Monero project introduced P2Pool, a mining pool running on a <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/side-chain\">sidechain</a> that gives participants full control of their node as with solo mining configurations.</p></div></div></div></div></div>", "polygon": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is Polygon (MATIC)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-polygon-matic\">Polygon</a> (previously Matic Network) is the first well-structured, easy-to-use platform for Ethereum scaling and infrastructure development. Its core component is Polygon SDK, a modular, flexible framework that supports building multiple types of applications.</p><p>To learn more about this project, check out our deep dive of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-polygon-matic\">Polygon Matic</a>.</p><p>Using Polygon, one can create <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/optimistic-rollups-for-the-rest-of-us\">optimistic rollup</a> chains, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/zero-knowledge-rollups\">ZK rollup</a> chains, stand alone chains or any other kind of infra required by the developer.</p><p>Polygon effectively transforms Ethereum into a full-fledged multi-chain system (aka Internet of Blockchains). This multi-chain system is akin to other ones such as Polkadot, Cosmos, Avalanche etc. with the advantages of Ethereum\u2019s security, vibrant ecosystem and openness.</p><p>The $MATIC token will continue to exist and will play an increasingly important role, securing the system and enabling governance.</p><p>Polygon (formerly Matic Network) is a <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/layer-2\">Layer 2</a> scaling solution backed by Binance and Coinbase. The project seeks to stimulate mass adoption of cryptocurrencies by resolving the problems of scalability on many blockchains.</p><p>Polygon combines the Plasma Framework and the proof-of-stake blockchain architecture. The Plasma framework used by Polygon as proposed by the co-founder of Ethereum, Vitalik Buterin, allows for the easy execution of scalable and autonomous smart contracts.</p><p>Nothing will change for the existing ecosystem built on the Plasma-POS chain. With Polygon, new features are being built around the existing proven technology to expand the ability to cater to diverse needs from the developer ecosystem. Polygon will continue to develop the core technology so that it can scale to a larger ecosystem.</p><p>Polygon boasts of up to 65,000 transactions per second on a single side chain, along with a respectable block confirmation time of less than two seconds. The framework also allows for the creation of globally available decentralized financial applications on a single foundational blockchain.</p><p>The Plasma framework gives Polygon the potential of housing an unlimited number of decentralized applications on their infrastructure without experiencing the normal drawbacks common on proof-of-work blockchains. So far, Polygon has attracted more than 50 DApps to its PoS-secured Ethereum sidechain.</p><p>MATIC, the native tokens of Polygon, is an <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/erc-20\">ERC-20</a> token running on the Ethereum blockchain. The tokens are used for payment services on Polygon and as a settlement currency between users who operate within the Polygon ecosystem. The transaction fees on Polygon <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/side-chain\">sidechains</a> are also paid in MATIC tokens.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of Polygon?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Polygon (formerly Matic Network) was launched in October 2017. Polygon was co-founded by Jaynti Kanani, Sandeep Nailwal and Anurag Arjun, two experienced blockchain developers and a business consultant.</p><p>Before moving to its network in 2019, the Polygon team was a huge contributor in the Ethereum ecosystem. The team worked on implementing the Plasma MVP, the WalletConnect protocol and the widely-used Dagger event notification engine on Ethereum.</p><p>The team included co-founder of Polygon, Jaynti Kanani. Jaynti, a full-stack developer and blockchain engineer currently serves as the CEO of Polygon.</p><p>Jaynti played an integral role in implementing Web3, Plasma and the WalletConnect protocol on Ethereum. Prior to his blockchain involvement, Jaynti worked as a data scientist with Housing.com.</p><p>Co-founder and chief operations officer of Polygon, Sandeep Nailwal is a blockchain programmer and entrepreneur. Before jointly starting Polygon (formerly Matic), Sandeep had served as the CEO of Scopeweaver, and the chief technical officer of Welspun Group.</p><p>Anurag Arjun is the only non-programming co-founder of Polygon. As a product manager, he has had stints with IRIS Business, SNL Financial, Dexter Consultancy and Cognizant Technologies.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes Polygon Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Polygon is self-described as a Layer 2 scaling solution, which means that the project doesn\u2019t seek to upgrade its current basic blockchain layer any time soon. The project focuses on reducing the complexity of scalability and instant blockchain transactions.</p><p>Polygon uses a customized version of the Plasma framework which is built on<a href=\"http://https:%2F%2Fblog.coinmarketcap.com%2F2018%2F10%2F19%2Fa-short-primer-on-proof-of-stake%2F/\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\" target=\"_blank\"> proof-of-stake</a> checkpoints that run through the Ethereum main-chain. This unique technology allows each sidechain on Polygon to achieve up to 65,536 transactions per block.</p><p>Commercially, the sidechains of Polygon are structurally designed to support a variety of decentralized finance (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-decentralized-finance\">DeFi</a>) protocols available in the Ethereum ecosystem.</p><p>While Polygon currently supports only Ethereum basechain, the network intends to extend support for additional basechains, based on community suggestions and consensus. This would make Polygon an interoperable decentralized Layer 2 blockchain platform</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many Polygon (MATIC) Tokens Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>MATIC tokens are released on a monthly basis. MATIC currently has a circulating supply of 4,877,830,774 MATIC tokens and a max supply of 10,000,000,000 MATIC tokens.</p><p>At its initial private sale in 2017, 3.8 percent of MATIC\u2019s max supply was issued. In the April 2019 launchpad sale, another 19 percent of the total supply was sold. The MATIC price was $0.00263 per token, and $5 million was generated.</p><p>The remaining MATIC tokens are distributed as follows:</p><ul><li>Team tokens: 16 percent of the total supply.</li><li>Advisors tokens: 4 percent of the total supply.</li><li>Network Operations tokens: 12 percent of the total supply.</li><li>Foundation tokens: 21.86 percent of the total supply.</li><li>Ecosystem tokens: 23.33 percent of the total supply.</li></ul><p>According to the release schedule, all the tokens will be released by December 2022.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the Polygon Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>As a<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/headlines/news/ethereum-layer-2-scaling-solution-optimism-preliminary-mainnet-january-15/\"> Layer 2 solution</a> utilizing a network of proof-of-stake validators for asset security, staking is an integral part of the Polygon ecosystem. Validators on the network will stake their MATIC tokens as collateral to become part of the network\u2019s PoS consensus mechanism and will receive MATIC tokens in return.</p><p>Members of the network who do not wish to become validators can delegate their MATIC tokens to another validator, but will still take part in their staking process and earn staking rewards.</p><p>In addition to the proof-of-stake checkpointing, Polygon uses block producers at the block producer layer to achieve a higher degree of decentralization. These block producers give finality to the main chains using checkpoints and fraud-proof mechanisms.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy Polygon (MATIC)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Being one of the projects that contributed a lot to the development of the Ethereum ecosystem, MATIC is popular among online exchanges focused on DeFi. The upgrade will completely change the way the fee mechanism works on the Ethereum network \u2014 it eliminates first-price auction as the main fee calculation mechanism and instead uses a base fee that is burned, instead of sent to miners. Although it does not lower transaction fees, it makes it more stable, allowing users to estimate costs better and reduce overpayment.</p><p>However, as MATIC tokens are burned as base fees \u2014 and MATIC has a fixed supply of 10 billion tokens \u2014 it will have a deflationary effect on the digital asset. Polygon\u2019s core team projected an annual burn of MATIC amounting to 0.27% of the token\u2019s total supply \u2014 around 27 million tokens. This deflationary pressure will most likely benefit validators and delegators the most, as rewards for processing transactions on Polygon are denominated in MATIC. Furthermore, base fee will increase automatically once the block is filled up, resulting in fewer spam transactions and less network congestion. Ethereum mainnet\u2019s <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/ethereums-london-hard-fork-goes-live\">London Hard Fork went live</a> on Aug. 5, 2021.</p></div></div></div></div></div>", "shiba-inu": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is SHIBA INU (SHIB)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>SHIB is the main token of the Shiba Inu ecosystem, bringing the power of a decentralized, community-led currency to millions across the globe. Since its inception in late 2020, the Ethereum-based SHIB token has grown to become a worldwide phenomenon, and is now accepted as a form of payment at hundreds of locations, either directly or through third-party intermediaries.</p><p>Shiba Inu coin was created anonymously in August 2020 under the pseudonym \"Ryoshi.\" Ryoshi says about himself that he is a nobody and not important and that the efforts to unmask his identity, even if successful, would be underwhelming.</p><p>This <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/memecoin\">meme coin</a> quickly gained speed and value as a community of investors was drawn in by the cute charm of the coin paired with headlines and tweets from personalities like Elon Musk and Vitalik Buterin. Vitalik Buterin was long believed to be the originator of Shiba Inu, but denied such rumors on the Lex Fridman podcast on June 5, 2021.</p><p>Since release SHIB now trades on the ecosystem's proprietary DEX, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/shibaswap/\">ShibaSwap</a>.</p><p>On Sept. 17, 2021, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/coinbase-exchange/\">Coinbase</a>, the largest U.S.-based crypto exchange, listed Shiba Inu on their platform. This news caused Shiba Inu price to rise by over 40% in the following two days, bringing the meme dog token into the spotlight again.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of SHIBA INU?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The SHIBA INU WoofPaper has three reasons why their team created SHIB:</p><ol start=\"1\"><li>\"We started from zero, with zero.\"</li><li>\"The brilliant minds behind Shib had never collaborated before.\"</li><li>\"We love Shiba Inu Dogs.\"</li></ol><p>The anonymous creator of the Shiba Inu coin is known as \"Ryoshi.\" However, very little is known of the mystery founder of the dog-themed cryptocurrency, much like the founder of Bitcoin, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/satoshi-nakamoto\">Satoshi Nakamoto</a>.</p><p>In his blog RYOSHI RESEARCH, he characterizes himself as \"just some guy of no consequence tapping at a keyboard.\" Ryoshi said that usually in projects there are different roles like a CEO, a \"tech guy,\" and a roadmap, resulting in \"someone plebs can bitch at.\" He stresses that with Shiba, no one person is accountable or responsible and underlines that he owns 0 SHIB to this day. For this reason, Ryoshi can be \"pure and unbiased,\" getting satisfaction from Shiba \"in other ways.\"</p><p>It has been speculated that Vitalik Buterin was behind the initial liquidity that helped set up Shiba Inu's liquidity on Uniswap. According to Ryoshi, he had \"a fren\" he met at Devcon in Osaka that sent him 10 ETH to set up the liquidity pair on Uniswap. Ryoshi also stated that Shiba Inu was an experiment in decentralized community building, and he thus declined all the influencer requests and pitches from different exchanges he received. His \"job\" is to defend the brand and give suggestions, although he does so very sparingly, as his last blog entry dates back to May 2021.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes SHIBA INU Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The SHIBA INU website invites dog-inspired artists from all over the world to foster the \"artistic Shiba movement\" as they bring their SHIBA INU community into the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/how-to-protect-your-nfts\">NFT market</a>. SHIBA INU has also created a campaign using Amazon Smile in order to collect donations to escue real, live Shiba Inu dogs with the Shiba Inu Rescue Association.</p><p>After initially being only one meme coin of many, Shiba Inu skyrocketed to popularity after Vitalik Buterin famously burned his share of the SHIB supply. Ryoshi had given Buterin 50% of the SHIB supply, announcing that \"as long as Vitalik doesn't rug us,\" Shiba Inu would be fine.</p><p>However, Buterin decided to burn 90% of his share, which later would have been worth billions thanks to the soaring value of SHIB. The remaining 10% were sent to a charity, as were about 50 trillion SHIB more that Vitalik had donated to a COVID-19 relief fund. He stated that he did not want \"to be a locus of power\" and thus gave the tokens away. This resulted in a temporary loss of value for SHIB, which the token later recovered from after the community agreed on an arrangement with the charity in question.</p><p>Ryoshi's goal for Shiba Inu has been to see if a perpetual decentralized organization could work with no central leadership. In a blog post, Royshi noted that the rift caused by Buterin's token donation made the community stronger and would enable it to distribute further and decentralize the movement. His vision for the core ecosystem is to perform its utility while the Shiba Inu-own stablecoin becomes the globalized exchange of value.</p><p>In October 2021, SHIB surged on the news of a possible Robinhood listing and briefly flipped Dogecoin to become the most-valued meme coin by market capitalization. Thus far, Robinhood has not listed SHIB, despite a petition with over 500,000 signatures calling for it. Robinhood executive Christine Brown has lauded the efforts of the Shiba Inu community, saying that one of her favorite things was seeing it engage with the community to make its wishes heard. However, Robinhood would prioritize safety over the \"short-term gain\" of a new token listing and has left Shiba Inu fans waiting since.</p><p>The October 2021 price surge famously minted a billionaire, as one wallet was uncovered that had bought $8,000 worth of SHIB in summer 2020, which was worth over $5.7 billion at SHIB's all-time high valuation. The wallet owner has not been determined, although the person appears to have sent parts of their fortune to other wallets several weeks after the price explosion.</p><p>The price surge also led to increased adoption across token holders. WhaleStats compiled data of the largest ETH wallets and found that SHIB represents over 20% of the combined market shares of all <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/erc-20\">ERC-20</a> tokens held by Ethereum whales. <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/crypto-com-coin/\">CRO</a> was a distant second with only 5%. SHIB also surpassed the one-million holder mark following its all-time high.</p><p>Moreover, retailers increasingly started adopting SHIB as a means of payment following its popularity among small-time investors. American electronics retailer Newegg added SHIB at the start of December 2021, partnering with crypto payments platform BitPay to unlock payments in SHIB. This followed the adoption of SHIB by over 500 merchants, according to payments firm CoinGate, with even Samsung-backed digital wallet provider ZenGo adding SHIB to its options and a <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/shiba-inu-accepted-at-restaurant-in-paris\">restaurant in Paris </a>accepting it as a payment option. At one point, the Shiba Inu community called for McDonald's to accept Shiba Inu, although the social media effort eventually fell short.</p><p>A major reason for the surging price of SHIB was a continued effort by the SHIB community to build a utility for the Shiba Inu token and the subsequent emergence of an entire Shiba Inu ecosystem.</p><p>ShibaSwap is the coin's designated DEX that started as a fork of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/sushiswap/\">Sushiswap</a> that has, in the words of Ryoshi, its \"own little twists and elements.\" Furthermore, Shiba Inu also plans to develop SHI, which will be the \"global exchange of value for plebs,\" an <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/algorithmic-stablecoin\">algorithmic stablecoin</a> pegged to one cent instead of one dollar as most other stablecoins. Its launch is planned after the Shiba <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/layer-2\">layer-two</a> solution called Shibarium, and Ryoshi envisions SHI to work in a similar way to <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/multi-collateral-dai/\">DAI</a>. That way, SHI would have collateral as a backstop that would push it back to one cent if the peg was lost.</p><p>According to Ryoshi, the end goal is that SHI becomes a global stable currency \"that plebs across all countries are able to use as both a store of value and method of payment.\"</p><p>In addition to SHI, a financial ecosystem is planned, and SHI would be added as a weighted pool pair on <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/curve-finance/\">Curve</a>. In that case, Ryoshi expects forks of the major DeFi protocols to appear in the Shiba Inu ecosystem, which would require an immutable bridge to function.</p><p>Shiba would also start hosting localized meetups and a once-a-year ShibaCon convention that would be hosted at an easily accessible location in a country without oppressive visa restrictions \"for the sake of inclusiveness for global plebs.\"</p><p>One immediate change Shiba Inu has implemented is increasing token burns, which have sparked renewed interest in the token at the beginning of 2022. Bigger Entertainment, a crypto record label selling merch, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/how-to-mint-an-nft\">NFTs</a> and concert tickets, organized a SHIB burn party that burned over 239 million SHIB over Christmas. In total, the team has burned almost one billion SHIB since the end of October.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many SHIBA INU (SHIB) Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The SHIBA INU website notes that they locked 50% of the total token supply on Uniswap, and \"threw away the keys!\" The remaining 50% was \"burned to Vitalik Buterin.\" In response to the \"gift\" from the Shiba Inu team, Vitalik Buterin sent 50 trillion SHIB tokens, worth $1 billion in Shiba Inu price at that time, to India's Covid Crypto Relief Fund. Buterin then <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/burned\">burned</a> 40% of the total supply to a dead wallet.</p><p>There are several other tokens described on the SHIBA INU website \u2014 LEASH, which has \"been unleashed and will not rebase,\" and BONE, the \"Dogecoin Killer.\" LEASH has a fixed supply of only 107,646 tokens, and offers enticing rewards to <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/liquidity-provider\">liquidity providers</a>, while BONE has 250,000,000 tokens, and is a <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/governance-token\">governance token</a> that allows holders to vote on the Shiba Inu's Doggy <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/decentralized-autonomous-organizations-dao\">decentralized autonomous organization</a> (DAO).</p><p>The WoofPaper notes that you will use SHIB to DIG for BONES or ShibaSwap, or even BURY your tokens. \"Trainers\" can teach their Shibas to SWAP tokens as well \u2014 all of these actions create \"Returns\" that are put into the Puppy Pools, where the #SHIBARMY has the option of BURYING or DIGGING for BONES.</p><p>At the beginning of May 2021, dog-themed meme tokens like Shiba Inu <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/ethereum-fees-hit-aths-amid-uncanny-dog-token-frenzy-a-data-perspective-by-intotheblock\">saw transaction volumes</a> in the hundreds of millions of dollars. Shiba Inu price hit an <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/all-time-high\">all-time high</a> (ATH) of 0.00005 on May 10, 2021, before going on a downtrend since.</p><p>As mentioned above, on May 13, Vitalik Buterin (who was given half of the token supply by the developers) <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/the-surprising-reason-shiba-inu-has-plunged-44-in-24-hours\">announced</a> that he was donating a large amount of these tokens to a fund helping India with COVID relief. The SHIBA developers had not anticipated Buterin selling his tokens, but eventually, the two parties came to a mutually satisfying agreement. Later, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/covid-fund-lost-1-2b-by-selling-shib-too-early\">the fund actually lamented having sold its tokens too early</a>, as its share would have been worth well over $1 billion at the token's all-time high.</p><p>Despite rumors alleging the contrary, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/shib-crashes-as-musk-reveals-which-coins-he-owns\">Elon Musk</a> does not own any SHIB. He confirmed as much in a tweet, which caused a temporary price drop.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the SHIBA INU Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>According to 22-page-long SHIB's WoofPaper, SHIB is an <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/erc-20\">ERC-20</a> token based on <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/ethereum/\">Ethereum</a>, a proof-of-work blockchain currently transitioning to proof-of-stake.</p><p>Ryoshi announced in his final blog post to date that Shiba Inu would develop its own layer-two solution that would be more decentralized than  <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/polygon/\">Polygon</a> or <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/binance-coin/\">BSC</a>, both of which Ryoshi regards as not truly decentralized. The Shiba L2 would be called \"Shibarium\" and is supposed to use BONE as its primary pair token, as written above.</p><p>According to Ryoshi, Shibarium would be built by a \"very competent blockchain team\" with experience building such solutions. Developer Eric M has announced in the Shiba Inu Discord server that Shibarium would launch \"soon,\" although he did not specify a date.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy SHIBA INU (SHIB)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>It is possible to buy Shiba Inu on <a href=\"https://www.binance.com/en/price/shiba-inu\">Binance</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/huobi-global/\">Huobi</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/coinbase-exchange/\">Coinbase</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/gate-io/\">Gate.io</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/uniswap-v2/\">Uniswap (V2)</a> and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/okex/\">OKEx</a>, among other exchanges.</p><p>To check Shiba Inu price live in the fiat currency of your choice, you can use CoinMarketCap's converter feature directly on the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/shiba-inu/\">Shiba Inu currency page</a>.
