While the idea and initial work on the project began in 2017, Solana was officially launched in March 2020 by the Solana Foundation with headquarters in Geneva, Switzerland.</p><p>To learn more about this project, check out our deep dive of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/solana\">Solana</a>.</p><p>The Solana protocol is designed to facilitate decentralized app (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/decentralized-applications-dapps\">DApp</a>) creation. It aims to improve scalability by introducing a proof-of-history (PoH) consensus combined with the underlying proof-of-stake (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/proof-of-stake-pos\">PoS</a>) consensus of the blockchain.</p><p>Because of the innovative hybrid consensus model, Solana enjoys interest from small-time traders and institutional traders alike. A significant focus for the Solana Foundation is to make decentralized finance accessible on a larger scale.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of Solana?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/anatoly-yakovenko/\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Anatoly Yakovenko</a> is the most important person behind Solana. His professional career started at Qualcomm, where he quickly moved up the ranks and became senior staff engineer manager in 2015. Later on, his professional path shifted, and Yakovenko entered a new position as a software engineer at Dropbox.</p><p>In 2017, Yakovenko started working on a project which would later materialize as Solana. He teamed up with his Qualcomm colleague <a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/gregoryrfitzgerald/\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Greg Fitzgerald</a>, and they founded a project called Solana Labs. Attracting several more former Qualcomm colleagues in the process, the Solana protocol and SOL token were released to the public in 2020.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes Solana Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>One of the essential innovations Solana brings to the table is the proof-of-history (PoH) consensus developed by Anatoly Yakovenko. This concept allows for greater scalability of the protocol, which in turn boosts usability.</p><p>Solana is known in the cryptocurrency space because of the incredibly short processing times the blockchain offers. Solana\u2019s hybrid protocol allows for significantly decreased validation times for both transaction and smart contract execution. With lightning-fast processing times, Solana has attracted a lot of institutional interest as well.</p><p>The Solana protocol is intended to serve both small-time users and enterprise customers alike. One of Solana\u2019s main promises to customers is that they will not be surprised by increased fees and taxes. The protocol is designed in such a way as to have low transaction costs while still guaranteeing scalability and fast processing.</p><p>Combined with the longstanding professional expertise creators Anatoly Yakovenko and Greg Fitzgerald bring to the project, Solana is ranked number 7 in the CoinMarketCap <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/\">ranking</a> as of September 2021.</p><p>This came on the back of an impressive bull run, where Solana price gained over 700% since mid-July 2021. The launch of the Degenerate Ape <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/how-to-mint-an-nft\">NFT collection</a> sent SOL price to an <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/all-time-high\">all-time high</a> (ATH) above $60, and it has been climbing since, largely due to higher developer activity on the Solana ecosystem, greater institutional interest, growing DeFi ecosystem, and the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/how-to-protect-your-nfts\">rise of the NFTs</a> and gaming vertical on Solana. Solana price rose to an ATH of $216 on Sept. 9, 2021.</p><p>Solana has received much praise for its speed and performance, and has even been tipped as a rival that can <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/solana-vs-ethereum-a-detailed-comparison\">compare to Ethereum</a> and challenge the dominant smart contract platform. However, the network has been plagued by repeated <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/solana-fastest-blockchain-in-world-hit-by-attack\">outages</a> that have impaired its price and aspirations to be the \"<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/solana-can-be-visa-of-crypto-bank-of-america-says\">Visa of crypto</a>.\" Furthermore, its <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-solana-a-guide-to-solana-s-ecosystem-projects\">ecosystem</a> is accused of favoring venture capital investors with unfair tokenomics.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many Solana (SOL) Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The Solana Foundation has announced that a total of 489 million SOL tokens will be released in circulation. At the moment, about 260 million of these have already entered the market.</p><p>The SOL token distribution is as follows: 16.23% went towards an initial seed sale, 12.92% of tokens were dedicated to a founding sale, 12.79% of SOL coins were distributed among team members and 10.46% of tokens were given to the Solana Foundation. The remaining tokens were already released for public and private sales or are still to be released to the market.</p><p>Solana price during the initial seed sale, held on April 5, 2018, was $0.04. Given the recent ATH, that represents an impressive 5400X <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/roi\">return on investment</a> (ROI).</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the Solana Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Solana relies on a unique combination of proof-of-history (PoH) and proof-of-stake (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/proof-of-stake-pos\">PoS</a>) consensus mechanisms.</p><p>Proof-of-history is the main component of the Solana protocol, as it is responsible for the bulk of transaction processing. PoH records successful operations and the time that has passed between them, thus ensuring the trustless nature of the blockchain.</p><p>The proof-of-stake (PoS) consensus is used as a monitoring tool for the PoH processes, and it validates each sequence of blocks produced by it.</p><p>The combination of two consensus mechanisms makes Solana a unique phenomenon in the blockchain industry.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy Solana (SOL)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>SOL tokens can be purchased on most exchanges. One choice to trade Solana is on <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/binance/\">Binance</a>, as it has the highest SOL/USDT trading volume, $753,103,225 as of September 2021.</p><p>Next is <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/coinbase-exchange/\">Coinbase</a>, with a trading volume of $343,872,841. Other options to trade Solana include <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/bilaxy/\">Bilaxy</a> and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/huobi-global/\">Huobi Globa</a>l. Of course, it is important to note that investing in cryptocurrency comes with a risk, just like any other investment opportunity.</p><p>To check Solana price live in the fiat currency of your choice, you can use CoinMarketCap\u2019s converter feature directly on the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/solana/\">Solana currency page</a>, or the dedicated exchange rate <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/converter/\">converter page</a>. Popular Solana price pairs include: <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/converter/sol/usd/\">SOL/USD</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/converter/sol/gbp/\">SOL/GBP</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/solana/sol/aud/\">SOL/AUD</a>,\n<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/converter/sol/jpy/\">SOL/JPY</a> and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/solana/sol/eur/\">SOL/EUR</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div>", "tron": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is TRON (TRX)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>TRON (TRX) is a decentralized blockchain-based operating system developed by the Tron Foundation and launched in 2017. Originally TRX tokens were <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/erc-20\">ERC-20</a>-based tokens deployed on <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/ethereum/\">Ethereum</a>, but a year later they were moved to their own network.</p><p>Initially, the project was created with the aim of providing full ownership rights to makers of digital content. The main goal is to help content creators (who receive only a small part of the income) and encourage them with more rewards for their work. How: invite content consumers to reward content makers directly (without intermediaries like YouTube, Facebook or Apple).</p><p>The TRON software supports <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/smart-contract\">smart contracts</a>, various kinds of blockchain systems, and decentralized applications aka dApps. The cryptocurrency platform uses a transaction model similar to <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/bitcoin/\">Bitcoin (BTC)</a>, namely UTXO. Transactions take place in a public ledger, where users can track the history of operations.</p><p>Therefore, the platform was built to create a decentralized Internet and serves as a tool for developers to create dApps, acting as an alternative to Ethereum. Anyone can create <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/decentralized-applications-dapps\">dApps</a> on the TRON network, offer content, and in return receive digital assets as compensation for their efforts. The ability to create content and share it openly without hesitation regarding transaction fees is an undeniable advantage of TRON.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of TRON?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>TRON was founded by Justin Sun, who now serves as CEO. Educated at Peking University and the University of Pennsylvania, he was recognized by Forbes Asia in its 30 Under 30 series for entrepreneurs.</p><p>Born in 1990, he was also associated with Ripple in the past \u2014 serving as its chief representative in the Greater China area.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes TRON Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>TRON has positioned itself as an environment where content creators can connect with their audiences directly. By eliminating centralized platforms \u2014 whether they are streaming services, app stores or music sites \u2014 it is hoped that creators won\u2019t end up losing as much commission to middlemen. In turn, this could also make content less expensive for consumers. Given how the entertainment sector is increasingly becoming digitized, TRON could have a headstart in applying blockchain technology to this industry.</p><p>The company also says that it has a talented and experienced developer team, based around the world, that has been drawn from major companies such as Ripple Labs.</p><p>Last but not least, whereas some other blockchain projects can be opaque about their plans for development, TRON offers a point of difference by delivering a roadmap that shows its intentions for the coming years.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many TRON (TRX) Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>TRON has a total supply of just over 100 billion tokens \u2014 and at the time of writing, about 71.6 billion of these are in circulation.</p><p>When a token sale was held in 2017, 15.75 billion TRX was allocated to private investors, while an additional 40 billion were earmarked for initial coin offering participants. The Tron Foundation was given 34 billion, and a company owned by Justin Sun got 10 billion.</p><p>All in all, this meant that 45% of TRX supply went to the founder and the project itself, while 55% was distributed among investors. Critics argue that this is a much higher ratio than what has been seen with other cryptocurrency projects.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the TRON Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>TRON uses a consensus mechanism that is known as <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/delegated-proof-of-stake-dpos\">delegated proof-of-stake</a>.</p><p>TRX owners can freeze their cryptocurrency in order to get Tron Power, which means that they can vote for \u201csuper representatives\u201d who serve as block producers.</p><p>These block producers receive TRX rewards in exchange for verifying transactions, and these rewards are then distributed among the people who voted for them.</p><p>According to TRON, this approach helps its blockchain to achieve higher levels of throughput.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy TRON (TRX)?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>It is possible to <a href=\"https://www.binance.com/en/buy-TRON\">buy Tron</a> from dozens of the exchanges it is listed on - including Poloniex, Bancor, KuCoin, Binance, Bitfinex, Coinbene and others. However, it is not supported by Coinbase.</p><p>Learn about converting your<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/how-to-buy-bitcoin/\"> fiat to Bitcoin here</a> \u2014 the perfect gateway to purchasing altcoins.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Network principles:</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The data hosted on the TRON network is free with no central authority. Content creators receive TRX tokens - a reward for their intellectual labour;</p><p>TRON supports the creation of coins by content makers, which can be used in their own developed applications;</p><p>TRON also carries out decentralized games on the network, players can encourage and reward creators with digital assets directly.</p><p>The ecosystem is based on three levels, which ensure the smooth and powerful operation of TRON. The architecture is as follows:</p><ul><li>Storage Layer, where network data, blockchain state and history data are securely stored. In general, its purpose is to segment all kinds of ecosystem data;</li><li>Application Layer, where developers are key figures and where TRX is utilized to develop applications and create wallets;</li><li>Core Layer, where various instructions are processed (which can be written only in two programming languages \u200b\u200b- Solidity and Java). Principle of operation: the core layer computes instructions, processes them, and sends them to the Tron Virtual Machine, where the logic happens, and dApps are executed.</li></ul><p>The main network protection tool, as well as one of the special features, is a delegated Proof-of-Stake (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/delegated-proof-of-stake-dpos\">dPoS</a>) system, an alternative to the Proof-of-Stake and Proof-of-Work consensus algorithms. This is a competitive advantage of TRON, because it means that the network is far more energy-efficient. Furthermore, due to its layered architecture, TRON processes more transactions at once than Proof-of-Work (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/proof-of-work-vs-proof-of-stake\">PoW</a>) systems. According to the development team, TRON has the higher throughput and is able to process up to 2000 operations per second without fees, thus, transactions on the network are feeless.</p><p>TRON is a blockchain-based operating system that aims to ensure this technology is suitable for daily use. Whereas Bitcoin can handle up to six transactions per second, and Ethereum up to 25, TRON claims that its network has capacity for 2,000 TPS.</p><p>To learn more about this project, check out our deep dive of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-tron\">Tron</a>.</p><p>This project is best described as a decentralized platform focused on content sharing and entertainment \u2014 and to this end, one of its biggest acquisitions was the file sharing service BitTorrent back in 2018.</p><p>Overall, TRON has divided its goals into six phases. These include delivering simple distributed file sharing, driving content creation through financial rewards, allowing content creators to launch their own personal tokens and decentralizing the gaming industry.</p><p>TRON is also one of the most popular blockchains for building <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/decentralized-applications-dapps\">DApps</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">USDD Stablecoin</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>In April 2022, the CEO of Tron, Justin Sun, announced plans to launch an <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/algorithmic-stablecoin\">algorithmic stablecoin</a>, dubbed Decentralized USD or <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/usdd/\">USDD</a>. It requires an automated balancing technique that burns $1 worth of TRX to mint 1 USDD. Tron DAO Reserve is responsible for managing USDD and ensuring that its value is stable relative to the value of its underlying collateral. Also, it sets the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/annual-percentage-yield-apy\">APY</a> offered to users <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/staking\">staking</a> USDD. At the time of writing, users earn a 30% yield on staked USDD.</p><p>While USDD has been criticized for borrowing heavily from the design of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/terrausd/\">UST</a> \u2014 <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/terra-luna/\">Terra</a>\u2019s algorithmic stablecoin which set off what was essentially a bank run and crash of the Terra ecosystem \u2014 certain elements set it apart. Perhaps the most notable is the decision to opt for a guaranteed over-collateralized framework, in contrast to the undercollateralized model of UST. The cryptocurrencies used as collateral on the USDD protocol include Tron, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/bitcoin/\">Bitcoin</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/usd-coin/\">USDC</a> and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/tether/\">Tether</a>.</p><p>The minimum collateral ratio of USDD has been set at 130%. Hence, the value of collateral deposited in the protocol's cryptocurrency reserves would, in practice, be higher than the value of USDD in circulation. With this, the possibility of a sustained depeg of USDD could be perceived as low. Despite its 130% minimum collateral ratio, USDD is at the time of writing backed by collateral reserves collectively worth over thrice the value of USDD in circulation. For the Tron DAO Reserve, the goal is to build a $10 billion treasury to back the value of USDD.</p><p>Another core element that is key to the stability of USDD is the operation of Super Representatives, which are Tron's institutional partners. The super representatives are incentivized entities that influence either side of the trade to absorb the potential volatility of the price of USDD. For instance, when the price of USDD falls below $1, the super representatives burn part of their USDD holding to mint TRX. This will, in turn, bring the value of USDD to the target price.</p><p>However, all these stability mechanisms have not stopped USDD from facing its fair share of volatility as the stablecoin. In June 2022, it experienced a 9% fall in its price relative to the value of 1 USD. In response, Tron DAO Reserve infused $650 million worth of USDC into USDD's collateral reserve.</p></div></div></div></div></div>", "wrapped-bitcoin": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is Wrapped Bitcoin [WBTC]?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-wrapped-bitcoin\">Wrapped Bitcoin</a> is a tokenized version of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/bitcoin/\">Bitcoin</a> (BTC) that runs on the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/ethereum/\">Ethereum</a> (ETH) blockchain.</p><p>WBTC is compliant with <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/erc-20\">ERC-20</a> \u2014 the basic compatibility standard of the Ethereum blockchain \u2014 allowing it to be fully integrated into the latter\u2019s ecosystem of decentralized exchanges, crypto lending services, prediction markets and other ERC-20-enabled decentralized finance (<a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/what-is-decentralized-finance\">DeFi</a>) applications.</p><p>WBTC is also backed by Bitcoin at a 1:1 ratio via a network of automatically monitored merchants and custodians, ensuring that its price is pegged to Bitcoin at all times and allows users to transfer liquidity between the BTC and the ETH networks in a decentralized and autonomous manner.</p><p>Wrapped Bitcoin was first announced on October 26, 2018, and officially launched on January 31, 2019.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Are Wrapped Bitcoin Created?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The creation of Wrapped Bitcoin brings the world's leading cryptocurrency <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/bitcoin/\">Bitcoin</a> into the world of Ethereum's <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/defi\">DeFi</a> ecosystem. The WBTC token adheres to the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/erc-20\">ERC-20</a> token standard, with tokens created for those who want to convert BTC into WBTC.</p><p>All to-be-converted BTC is held by a custodian, who takes part in the actual minting and burning of Ethereum-based tokens. When WBTCs are burned, the user can reclaim their BTC balance from the custodian. During mining, users send BTC to the custodian for storage and receive an equivalent in WBTC tokens. BitGo is the biggest custodian for Wrapped Bitcoin, and they will mine a certain number of WBTC and send them to the merchant's Ethereum address.</p><p>The user who wants to swap between wBTC and BTC performs a trade \u2014 through a centralized exchange or atomic swap on a decentralized exchange \u2014 to move funds to the merchant. Once finalized, the user can use their BTC/wBTC as they see fit. If WBTC is converted to BTC, the associated Wrapped Bitcoin balance will be destroyed through a burn transaction.</p><p>The WBTC <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/decentralized-autonomous-organizations-dao\">DAO</a> consists of governing members who decide on significant upgrades and changes to the protocol. Additionally, these members can serve as merchants or custodians managing BTC assets.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Can You Do With WBTC?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>As Wrapped Bitcoin tokens adhere to the ERC-20 token standard, one can use them across the broader Ethereum ecosystem. That includes trading them on decentralized exchanges  \u2014 like <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/uniswap/\">Uniswap</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/1inch/\">1Inch</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/sushiswap/\">Sushiswap</a> \u2014 and exploring decentralized finance opportunities through protocols and platforms supporting WBTC.</p><p>DeFi opportunities for WBTC range from lending and borrowing to <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/yield-farming\">yield farming</a>, token swapping and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/glossary/liquidity-pool\">liquidity pools</a>. Various protocols and platforms support Wrapped Bitcoin, including <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/aave/\">Aave</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/balancer/\">Balancer</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/compound/\">Compound</a>, <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/maker/\">MakerDAO</a>. Some of these providers may issue platform-native governance tokens as an extra incentive.</p><p>Using WBTC as colateral for a crypto-backed loan can be a significant option for businesses. Additionally WBTC holders can earn interest from supplying liquidity, although the APY will be relatively low.</p><p>Another option for WBTC is to engage in margin trading, where Wrapped Bitcoin is used to margin trade <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/ethereum/\">Ethereum</a>, stablecoins and other ERC-20 tokens. Users deploy WBTC to enhance fund security while trading. That process is fully non-custodial and powered by smart contract technology.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of Wrapped Bitcoin?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The Wrapped Tokens project, of which WBTC is a part, wasn\u2019t founded by individuals but is rather a joint project of three organizations: BitGo, Kyber Network and <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/ren/\">Ren</a>.</p><p>BitGo, co-founded in 2013 by American computer scientist and entrepreneur Mike Belshe, is an institutional digital asset custody, trading and financial services firm. In addition to being one of the developers of WBTC, BitGo also serves as its original custodian \u2014 the entity that holds WBTC tokens and the keys needed to mint more of them.</p><p>Kyber Network is an on-blockchain liquidity protocol that enables the integration of different cryptocurrency tokens and DeFi applications. It was founded in 2017 by Loi Luu, Victor Tran and Yaron Velner and is based in Singapore. Along with Ren, Kyber Network has helped create WBTC and still serves as a merchant on its network \u2014 the institution that mints and burns WBTC tokens to maintain the 1:1 ratio of tokens to BTC reserves.</p><p>Similarly to Kyber, Ren is a company focused on cross-blockchain integration of cryptocurrency assets and DeFi applications via solutions such as RenBridge, RenVM and others. It was founded in 2017 by Taiyang Zhang and Loong Wang.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes Wrapped Bitcoin Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>By virtue of being the oldest and largest cryptocurrency on the market, Bitcoin can boast a massive user base and a liquidity pool of several dozen billion dollars. However, its blockchain functionality is relatively basic by modern standards.</p><p>Unlike Bitcoin, Ethereum was built from the ground up to support more advanced use cases by utilizing the technology of smart contracts, giving rise to an entire industry dubbed \u201cdecentralized finance.\u201d</p><p>Ethereum and products derived from it offer their users such advanced financial instruments as lending and insurance, which do not rely on trusted intermediaries.</p><p>By \u201cwrapping\u201d BTC in the ERC-20 standard, WBTC enables full integration of a Bitcoin-like asset into this advanced environment of financial decentralized applications, bringing along the immense liquidity associated with the BTC market.</p><p>In addition, Wrapped Bitcoin makes the job significantly easier for exchanges, wallets and payment services that work with Ethereum: instead of having to run two separate nodes for ETH and BTC networks, they can support WBTC operations with just an Ethereum node.</p><p>Finally, Ethereum blockchain\u2019s faster average blocktime \u2014 about 15 seconds vs 10 minutes respectively \u2014 increases the speed with which WBTC can be transacted, compared to actual bitcoins.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many Wrapped Bitcoin [WBTC] Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>There is no predetermined schedule of WBTC issuance. Instead, WBTC is automatically minted or burned whenever users purchase or sell their tokens for Bitcoin via a system of merchants and custodians.</p><p>Because Wrapped Bitcoin is always backed by Bitcoin at a 1:1 ratio, the number of tokens in circulation is directly dependent on the amount of Bitcoin reserves in the WBTC network. As of October 2020, that number was just over 94,000 tokens, worth approximately $1 billion in total.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the Wrapped Bitcoin Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>WBTC tokens are secured by the parent blockchain they run on \u2014 Ethereum. In turn, ETH is protected by the Ethash <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/proof-of-work-vs-proof-of-stake\">proof-of-work</a> function, a representative of the Keccak family of hash functions.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy Wrapped Bitcoin [WBTC]?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>You can buy WBTC on several exchanges, both centralized and decentralized ones, which serve as merchants on the Wrapped Bitcoin network. Some of the major ones include:</p><ul><li><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/uniswap-v2/\">Uniswap</a></li><li><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/binance/\">Binance</a></li><li><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/okex/\">OKEx</a></li><li><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/huobi-global/\">Huobi Global</a></li><li><a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/exchanges/kyber-network/\">Kyber Network</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Wrapped Bitcoin's Flow into Ethereum Network</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>Part of Bitcoin\u2019s circulating supply has flowed into the Ethereum Network, corporate treasuries and exchange-traded investment products in the form of wrapped BTC (WBTC) in 2021. <a href=\"https://twitter.com/ArcaneResearch/status/1473998005477036040\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">According to Arcane Research</a>, while Bitcoin balance on crypto exchanges has fallen by roughly 1.2%, Bitcoin held in corporate treasuries, exchange-traded investment vehicles and on Ethereum has risen by 0.51%, 0.69% and 0.98% respectively. There is currently <a href=\"https://wbtc.network/dashboard/order-book\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">$10.9B worth of WBTC</a> on the Ethereum network, as of February 2022. Besides Ethereum, WBTC is also available on the <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/currencies/tron/\">Tron blockchain</a>, with a total value of $4.1M worth of Bitcoin.</span></div></div></div></div>", "xrp": "<div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Is XRP / XRP Ledger?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronUp\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA show\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>Launched in 2021, the <a href=\"http://www.xrpl.org\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">XRP Ledger (XRPL)</a> is an open-source, permissionless and decentralized technology. Benefits of the XRP Ledger include its low-cost ($0.0002 to transact), speed  (settling transactions in 3-5 seconds), scalability (1,500 transactions per second) and inherently green attributes (carbon-neutral and energy-efficient). The XRP Ledger also features the first decentralized exchange (DEX) and custom tokenization capabilities built into the protocol. Since 2012, the XRP Ledger has been operating reliably, having closed 70 million ledgers.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Who Are the Founders of the XRP Ledger?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>In 2012, David Schwartz, Jed McCaleb and Arthur Britto launched the XRP Ledger with its native currency XRP as a faster, more energy-efficient alternative to the Bitcoin blockchain. In September that year, along with Chris Larsen, they founded the company that is today known as Ripple.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">What Makes XRPL Unique?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>The XRP Ledger presents a wide variety of applications and use cases related to payments including micropayments, DeFi, and, soon, NFTs. Deployed in 2012, the XRPL supports enterprises and Python, Java and JavaScript developers with powerful utility and flexibility. On the XRP website, developers can access different tutorials to help them get started using different coding languages, building apps, managing accounts and more.</p><p>Alongside its native coin, XRP, the XRP Ledger is used by developers to create solutions that solve inefficiencies, including remittance and asset tokenization. Currently, the five main applications of the XRP Ledger are payments, tokenization, DeFi, CBDCs and stablecoins.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Many XRP Coins Are There in Circulation?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><span>The XRP Ledger architects gifted 80 billion XRP to Ripple so that the company could build use cases \u2014 including its global payments network, RippleNet \u2014 around the digital asset.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">How Is the XRP Ledger Network Secured?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>Unlike Bitcoin or Ethereum, the XRPL uses a unique Federated Consensus mechanism as its method of validating transactions. Transactions are confirmed on the XRPL through a consensus protocol, in which designated independent servers called validators come to an agreement on the order and outcome of XRP transactions. All servers in the network process each transaction according to the same rules, and any transaction that follows the protocol is confirmed right away. All transactions are public and transparent, and anyone can operate a validator. There are currently over 150 validators on the ledger, operated by universities, exchanges, businesses, and individuals around the world.</p><p>Through the Federated Consensus mechanism, all verified transactions can be processed without a single point of failure as no single participant makes a decision independently.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-30065ccd-0 keBwNL\"><div class=\"readmoreDesc\" data-direction=\"ltr\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hAKSew top\"><h3 class=\"sc-16891c57-0 hTWugv base-text\">Where Can You Buy XRP?</h3><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 gPFIPZ right\"><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 viaWE\"><svg class=\"sc-16891c57-0 bbyRUs c-i\" height=\"1em\" loading=\"lazy\" version=\"1.1\" viewbox=\"0 0 24 24\" width=\"1em\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\"><use href=\"#chevronDown\"></use></svg></div></div></div><div class=\"sc-16891c57-0 igLZtA hidden\"><div class=\"sc-95c7b9b5-0 AaeSH\"><div><p>XRP is listed on many CeFi exchanges globally, including Binance, Huobi and Bitstamp.</p><p>To learn more about this project, check out our deep dive of <a href=\"https://coinmarketcap.com/alexandria/article/xrp-a-history\">XRP</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div>"}
